ã€6a1n60ldã€ - Immediately gives 100,000 yen and "Ruika's Magic Hammer" (cheat item), which increases drop rate
ã€healmeplzã€ - Gives "Mio's First Aid Kit" (cheat item) that massively restores health per second

ã€60dpatã€ - Gives you the "Catalyst Amatoria" equipment which makes headpats give 1 red heart immediately when worn
ã€muestaczã€ - Gives you the "Absolute Territory" equipment, which gives +99 weapon/equipment inventory space when worn
ã€1f0g0ty0uã€- sister's name will be forgotten and will let the player rename her. (does not count as cheat code)
ã€aut0updateã€- forces the game to update (MOBILE ONLY, does not count as a cheat code)

During RPG/Adventure Mode, there is no input box. Just type the codes in your keyboard and remember not to copy paste.

- Moving and dancing sideways will guarantee evasion on all attacks
- Spinning deflects most projectiles
- Will have an instant "teleportation" move that will almost instantly kill you (a reference to Street Fighter's Shun Goku Satsu)
- When bitten by ASABA, it will consume any food you have with you and restore its health. If it happens to consume bad food, it will become poisoned.

12. ãŠå…„ã¡ã‚ƒã‚“ã®æ”»æ’ƒåŠ›ãŒé«˜ã„ã»ã©ã€é›é€ ã®åŠ¹æœã‚‚é«˜ã¾ã‚Šã¾ã™ã€‚
13. æ­¦å™¨ã‚’æŒãŸãªã„ç´ æ‰‹ã®çŠ¶æ…‹ã§ã¯ã€é‰„ã®ç §ã‚’å¬å–šã™ã‚‹ã“ã¨ã¯ã§ãã¾ã›ã‚“ã€‚
14. å°†æ¥çš„ã«ã¯ã€æ­¦å™¨ã®åŠ¹æœã‚’å‘ä¸Šã•ã›ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã«ç£¨ãã‚„ã€ä»–ã®éæ­¦å™¨ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’ç½®ãã“ã¨ãŒã§ãã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã«ãªã‚‹äºˆå®šã§ã™ã€‚ã”æœŸå¾…ãã ã•ã„ã€‚ 		Regarding the "Anvil"
1. This will replace "Senpuu"(Dash). Using Senpuu will instead pull out an anvil so you can start forging. Your main weapon will automatically be unequipped and replaced with "Forging Hammer".
2. "Forging Hammer" has infinite durability and will be unequipped if you pick up the anvil or change maps.
3. Attacking the anvil with the hammer counts as "forging". Each strike you do increases the weapon's temperature, with higher temperatures leading to higher chance and higher value in restoring the weapon's durability
4. When there are enemies near the anvil, you will get additional rewards.
5. When the weapon starts to overheat, you need to wait for it to cooldown because striking it won't yield anything.
6. The repaired durability of the equipment can't exceed its original maximum cap
7. Forging can only be used on the ground
8. During forging, the anvil gets automatically picked up if the player dies. When you change maps, you always have to go back to the map where you placed the anvil to see it again. Reviving doesn't automatically pick up the anvil.
9. Currently, there are no designs for multiple types of anvils.
10. When a weapon reaches its max temperature and overheats, you can simple put it away and place it again to bypass the cooldown time
11. The Forging Hammer weapon itself also benefits from bonuses such as Neko Punch or "Weapon Enlargement" from tarot cards to improve forging effectiveness.
12. The higher your attack power, the greater the effects of forging is.
13. If you are unarmed (barehanded with no weapon equipped), the anvil can't be summoned
14. In the future, there will be features such as polishing to further enhance the weapons' effects or even put non-weapon items on the anvil. Stay tuned!		å…³äº"é“ç §"çš„è¯´æ˜

Detailed instructions for fishing:

NOTE: Everything resets when it rains

When a bomb is thrown in the water, the chance of a fish or item coming out is 5%. Rain significantly boosts the chance of this by 30%-50%

1. The number of fish or items that a surface of water is limited. The larger the body of water is, the more it can give up to a maximum of 50 drops.

2. When a Gachapon machine is directly spawned in the body of water or an enemy falls into the water, it will act as some sort of "fertilizer". This increases the drop rate on that body of water by 50% (broken Gachapon machine doesn't count). The amount of items/fish dropped is also increased along with your sin value.

3. Onii-chan's luck stat affects fishing, up to a maximum of 75% bonus chance.

4. If there are shadows of a fish in the body of water, directly attacking them or swimming to them will yield a fish drop. One time only per fish shadow.

5. Bubbles on the surface of water indicates the presence of an item. Throwing bombs to it or using the water staff can trigger them to get some drops. They have a higher chance of either spawning an enemy or drop an equipment. Fishes have a lower chance of dropping items.

6. Throwing a fertilizer on the surface of water will significantly boost the chances of an item/fish being obtained.

7. Living creatures that fall into the body of water will become "fertilizers", adding new drops, etc. including the Sacambaspis' that escapes to the water when thrown.

8. The TV show occassionally forecasts something related to fishing. This only changes the drop pool and not necessarily changes the drop rate or amount of drops.

9. Fertilizers thrown stack with each other as long as they're in range, cumulatively boosting the chances up to 100%, resulting into dropping special items or reeling in The River Lord boss.

10. If the body of water is very small, certain creatures won't spawn at all (such as bosses). If the land where the Sacambaspis' spawns is very small, it will immediately escape.

TLDR
Rainy weather, luck, gachapon machines in the water all make the ideal conditions for fishing. Both applicable on the large river in Forest of Ruins - 1 and the river in Forest of Ruins just above the starting area		å…³äºæ°´é¢ç‚¸é±¼çš„è¯¦ç»†è¯´æ˜(æ‰€æœ‰çš„é¡¹ç›®ï¼Œä¸‹é›¨çš†ä¼šé‡ç½®)ï¼š

When The River King's health drops below 90%, there's a chance where it will sleep to restore its health. Attacking it will wake it up.

Upon defeat, if there's a body of water in an 8-block radius, it will stop fighting and jump right back to the water. When this happens, it has a chance of dropping its crown (Royal Decree). If it was defeated under movement impairing debuffs (Paralyzed, Frozen or Stunned), it will still jump to the water but the chance of dropping the crown is significantly boosted.

If there's no water nearby, it will wither into a normal-sized Sacambaspis due to exhaustion, unable to escape, and will become a servant drop (â—‰â–½â—‰(Pink)). Despite this, it still has a chance to drop Royal Decree.		è¨å¡ç­ç”²é±¼ç‹è¡€é‡ä½äº90%æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰æœºç‡ç¡çœ å›å¤è¡€é‡ï¼Œå—åˆ°æ”»å‡»ä¼šé†’æ¥
